<analysis>**original_problem_statement:**
The user's initial request was for a complete overhaul of the Smart Project Builder application's pricing system. This evolved into a comprehensive full-stack enhancement project aimed at making the site go-live ready.

The scope expanded to include:
1.  A full analytics and tracking system.
2.  Comprehensive Arabic language support.
3.  Resolution of critical bugs and UI fixes.
4.  Implementation of A/B testing frameworks.
5.  An overhaul of the email notification system.
6.  Implementation of foundational and advanced SEO/UX features, with a major focus on creating numerous geo-targeted landing pages for the UAE, GCC, and other international markets.
7.  Creation of high-intent, service-specific SEO landing pages (e.g., High-End Audio, Home Theater).
8.  Site-wide performance and responsive design optimizations.
9.  New user engagement features like Dark Mode, Schedule a Visit, Recently Viewed items, and AI-powered Smart Recommendations.
10. WhatsApp conversion optimization with context-specific messaging.

PRODUCT REQUIREMENTS:
The user's direction is a multi-phase go-live checklist focusing on:
-   **Phase 1 (Must-Do):** Full tracking implementation, WhatsApp conversion optimization, and creating geo-targeted SEO pages.
-   **Phase 2 (Authority):** Adding social proof, enhancing partner portals, and building out the Experience Centre funnel.
-   **Phase 3 (Sales Intelligence):** Implementing automated lead routing, lead scoring, and a sales dashboard.

**User's preferred language**: English

**what currently exists?**
The application is a full-stack project with a Next.js frontend and a FastAPI backend. Key features include:
- An extensive set of 28 geo-targeted landing pages covering the UAE, GCC, and key cities in the Middle East and Africa, all managed by a backend API () and an admin panel.
- A dynamic sitemap () that automatically includes all database-driven pages.
- Several new high-intent SEO service pages (e.g., , ).
- Enhanced partner portals for Architects and Developers with new sections detailing partner programs and benefits.
- An optimized WhatsApp conversion system, featuring a reusable CTA component and context-aware, pre-filled messages on key pages.
- A centralized email service, analytics dashboard, and full Arabic language support.
